 2

 3

 4

 5

 6

 The Supreme Court today gave a major verdict allowing the 24-week pregnant rape victim of Mumbai to have an abortion
 court kaa kahana he ki agar mahila kii jaan ko khatra he to 20 hafte baad bhi garbhpaat karaayaa ja saktaa he
 The court has given this decision within the ambit of the law itself
 act kaa section 3 kahata he ki 20 hafte se zyada hone par garbhpaat nahin ho saktaa lekin section 5 kahata he ki agar mahila kii jaan ko khatra ho to kabhi bhi garbhpaat kiya ja saktaa he
 The Supreme Court has considered this case as Life vs Life and said that abortion can be done so that the life of the woman is in danger, but whether the 1971 law is right or not, the Supreme Court will continue to hear it
 ullekhneey he ki medical termination of pregnancy act 1971 ke mutabik 20 hafte se zyaada garbhvatee mahila kaa garbhpaat nahin ho saktaa
 The rape victim of Mumbai had challenged this act in the Supreme Court, calling it unconstitutional and sought permission to have an abortion
 mahila ne apni yachika main kaha he ki vah behad hi garib parivaar se he uske mangetar ne shaadi kaa jhansa dekar uske saath balaatkaar kiya or use dhokhaa dekar duusari ladki se shaadi kar lee, jiske baad usne mangetar ke khilaaf balaatkaar kaa cese darj kiya gaya
 When the woman came to know that she was pregnant, she underwent several medical tests, which showed that if she does not undergo an abortion, she can be killed
 2 june 2016 ko doctoron ne uskaa garbhpaat karne se inkaar kar diya kyonki use garbhadhaaran kiye 20 hafte se zyaada ho chuke the
 The woman said in her petition that when the law was enacted in 1971, the 20-week rule was correct at the time, but now the time has changed, now even after 26 weeks, abortion can happen
 isse purv supreme court ko mumbai ke KE medical aspataal ne report saunpi thi, jiske baad court ne yah faisla sunaaya
 During the hearing of the case on July 22, SG Ranjit Kumar, on behalf of the Central Government, suggested that a medical board be formed in the matter which would examine the woman and decide whether she could be miscarried
 iske liye AIIMS ke doctor kii ek team banaai jaae jo mahila kii jaanch karegi
 The comments lekin yachikakarta ke vakil ne kaha tha ki mahila mumbai he or vah dilli aane main sakasham nahin he
 In such a situation, it should be investigated in Mumbai itself
 tab maharashtra sarkaar ke vakil ne kaha tha ki mumbai ke KE medical aspataal main jaanch ho sakati he, jiske baad court ne report daakhil kii thi
